// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int choice;
    char inputFileName[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[     scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");

// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {

[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[];

    printf("File Compressor/Decompressor\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Compress a file\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Decompress a file\n");
    printf("Enter your choice ((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((( or                                                                                                                         ): ");
    scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");
            break;
    }

    return                                                                                                     ;
}
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int choice;

[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[];

    printf("File Compressor/Decompressor\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Compress a file\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Decompress a file\n");
    printf("Enter your choice ((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((( or                                                                                                                         ): ");
    scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");
            break;
    }

    return                                                                                                     ;
}
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int choice;

[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[];

    printf("File Compressor/Decompressor\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Compress a file\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Decompress a file\n");
    printf("Enter your choice ((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((( or                                                                                                                         ): ");
    scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");
            break;
    }

    return                                                                                                     ;
}
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int choice;

[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[];

    printf("File Compressor/Decompressor\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Compress a file\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Decompress a file\n");
    printf("Enter your choice ((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((( or                                                                                                                         ): ");
    scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");
            break;
    }

    return                                                                                                     ;
}
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int choice;

[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[];

    printf("File Compressor/Decompressor\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Compress a file\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Decompress a file\n");
    printf("Enter your choice ((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((( or                                                                                                                         ): ");
    scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");
            break;
    }

    return                                                                                                     ;
}
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int choice;

[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[];

    printf("File Compressor/Decompressor\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Compress a file\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Decompress a file\n");
    printf("Enter your choice ((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((( or                                                                                                                         ): ");
    scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");
            break;
    }

    return                                                                                                     ;
}
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int choice;

[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[];

    printf("File Compressor/Decompressor\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Compress a file\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Decompress a file\n");
    printf("Enter your choice ((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((( or                                                                                                                         ): ");
    scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");
            break;
    }

    return                                                                                                     ;
}
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int choice;

[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[];

    printf("File Compressor/Decompressor\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Compress a file\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Decompress a file\n");
    printf("Enter your choice ((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((( or                                                                                                                         ): ");
    scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");
            break;
    }

    return                                                                                                     ;
}
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int choice;

[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[[];

    printf("File Compressor/Decompressor\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Compress a file\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Decompress a file\n");
    printf("Enter your choice ((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((( or                                                                                                                         ): ");
    scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");
            break;
    }

    return                                                                                                     ;
}
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>

// Utility functions
void handleFileError(FILE *file, const char *fileName) {
    if (file == NULL) {
        printf("Error: Could not open file %s\n", fileName);
        exit((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((();
    }
}

// Function declarations
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName);

// Compression logic
void compressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    int count;
    char currentChar, nextChar;

    // Reading the first character
    currentChar = fgetc(inputFile);
    
    while (currentChar != EOF) {
        count =                                                                                                               ;
        nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);

        // Count consecutive occurrences of the same character
        while (nextChar == currentChar && nextChar != EOF) {
            count++;
            nextChar = fgetc(inputFile);
        }

        // Write the character and its count to the compressed file
        fprintf(outputFile, "%c%d", currentChar, count);

        // Update current character
        currentChar = nextChar;
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File compressed successfully!\n");
}

// Decompression logic
void decompressFile(const char *inputFileName, const char *outputFileName) {
    FILE *inputFile = fopen(inputFileName, "r");
    handleFileError(inputFile, inputFileName);

    FILE *outputFile = fopen(outputFileName, "w");
    handleFileError(outputFile, outputFileName);

    char currentChar;
    int count;

    // Read character and its count and write decompressed output
    while (fscanf(inputFile, "%c%d", &currentChar, &count) != EOF) {
        for (int i =                                                                                                     ; i < count; i++) {
            fputc(currentChar, outputFile);
        }
    }

    fclose(inputFile);
    fclose(outputFile);

    printf("File decompressed successfully!\n");
}

// Main function
int main() {
    int choice;

    printf("File Compressor/Decompressor\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Compress a file\n");
    printf(""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""". Decompress a file\n");
    printf("Enter your choice ((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((((( or                                                                                                                         ): ");
    scanf("%d", &choice);

    switch (choice) {
        case                                                                                                               :
            printf("Enter the input file name to compress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the compressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            compressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        case                                                                                                                         :
            printf("Enter the input file name to decompress: ");
            scanf("%s", inputFileName);
            printf("Enter the output file name for the decompressed file: ");
            scanf("%s", outputFileName);
            decompressFile(inputFileName, outputFileName);
            break;

        default:
            printf("Invalid choice. Please enter                                                                                                                or                                                                                                                         .\n");
            break;
    }

    return                                                                                                     ;
}
